 ' After eight years in India, Mithu Sen's solo show is "anamithu - Byproduct of 20 Years of Performance"
 yah pradarshnee mumbai kii chemold presscott road par 31 janvari se 8 march ke bich khuli thi
 Mithu was born in West Bengal in 1971 and studied painting at the Kala Bhavan Institute of Fine Art of Viswan Bharati University, Santiniketan
 unka samoochaa kaam us jindagi kaa aks he jo unhone ji he
 His work at the India Art Fair stood like a set of four books: the first three books have outstretched lips and the fourth has an iron press with a raised penis
 apni theme ke bare main ve kahati hai, ''main waisi hum jaise ''meri" asweekruti rahi he, har koi faisla suna detaa rahaa he ki mujhe kya hona chahie
 "sen speaks of his father jokingly saying that he would have to pay a huge dowry because of his dark complexion and even when a bus conductor in Mahabalipuram, Tamil Nadu asked him in local language They talked and when they told that they did not know this language, they came down on the abuses
 sen kahati hai ki ve apni kalakritiyon ko bhent karke kala kii duniya kii maang or supplai kii fitrat kaa muqabla karne kii koshish kar rahi hai
 "life is a medium for me," says Sen
 haas-parihaas us sagar kaa ek nanha-sa hissaa he
 i like to play with serious issues, so dilligi becomes a good tool for me to speak
 main apni hi kamajoriyon or bikli kaa istemaal karti hum
 When the audience laughs, that human sympathy breaks the barriers of the enormous issues with which i deal
 hansi-majaak logon ko sanjeeda chizon main laane kaa acha tarika he
 "she says," i use "non" as an ornament
 jab ise sangya, kriya visheshan or visheshan ke purv joda jaataa he, to yah us lafj ke myne ko ulat detaa he
 "non" is a linguistic tool that opens up layers of possible expressions of my work
 vah sab kuch ho saktaa he‚Äîsiyaasi, saamaajik, nijee, yonik, alangik
 It is a deliberate intervention with issues, so it is political
 main kah rahi hum ki ek pahchaan or tamaam (gaiyr) pahachaanen siyaasi hi hai
 "while she is blasting the language through her works in the exhibition, she says that she is also" paying attention to human relationships by reversing the established ways of communicating and thus to address the mind and human behavior
 " Vali exposes tangled and poppy layers of senses
 iskaa nateeja drawing, kavita, murtishilp or sthapaty kala kii shakl main saamne aata he jo unke kaam ke sahautpaada kii tarah hai

 Political background In the Godda Lok Sabha seat, there is a tough fight between the Congress and the BJP
 saal 1962 or 1967 ke chunaav main is seat se congress ke prabhudayal ne chunaav jeeta
 Jagdish Mandal won in 1971 and 1977
 saal 1971 main jagadish congress or 1977 main bhartiya lokdal ke tikat par lade the
 Maulana Saminuddin won from this seat in 1980 and 1984
 saal 1989 main is seat par bijepi ke janardan yadav jite
 Suraj Mandal of JMM won in 1991
 iske baad bijepi ne vaapasi kii
 Jagadambi Prasad Yadav won the 1996, 1998 and 1999 elections on a BJP ticket
 2000 kaa chunaav bijepi ke hi tikat par pradeep yadav jite
 In 2004, Congress returned and won Furkan Ansari on its ticket
 2009 or 2014 main bijepi ke nishikant doobe jite

 Space

 spes

 Sodium glucamate or monosodium glutamate is used in most foods
 restaurant main parose jane vaale bhojan main bhi is safed padaarth kaa jamkar istemaal hota he kyonki isse bhojan kaa swaad bad jaataa he
 It is naturally present in many foods but is also mixed separately in processed food
 sodium glutamet safed crystal powder kii tarah hota he or chini-namak se bahut miltaa-julata he
 Monosodium glutamate (MSG) is added to foods to enhance flavor
 bhale hi yah bhojan kaa swaad badha detaa ho lekin iske zyada seven se nerve system par bura asar padataa he
 Taking MSG in small amounts is safe, but for people who are allergic to it, consuming it in small amounts can also be dangerous
 dhyaan dene vaali baat ye he ki chips, packaged soup, canned food jaise processd food main MSG zyada maatra main maujuud hota he
 Processed foods are already harmful and cause further harm due to MSG
 aage kuch bhi kharidne se pehle packet par check kar len ki MSG maujuud he yaa nahin
 If the ingredient has MSG written then avoid eating it
 rasaynic taur par prakritik taur par khaane main paae jane vaale ems or processd food main maujuud MSG main koi fark nahin hota he
 But due to high amount of MSG in processed food or the presence of other harmful substances, it can prove more dangerous
 yah canned food, sos, chips, packet band soup, hot dog, bear jaisi chizon main hota he
 Apart from this, it is naturally present in cheese, tomatoes, peas, walnuts, wheat
 sodium glutamet kii zyada khuraaq ko bhukh badhane, motopa va anya metabolic disorder se jodakar dekha jaataa he
 Excess intake of sodium glutamate can cause problems like migraine, lethargy, hormone imbalance, vomiting, weakness, chest pain
 isse khaane kaa swaad bad jaataa he jisase log zyada kha lete hai
 The result is obesity and overweight
 sodium glutamet kaa brain koshikaon par drug kii tarah asar hota he
 Several studies have reported that diabetes cases have also increased due to increasing sodium glutamate intake
 iske zyada seven se adrenal granthi kii kriya par asar padataa he, hai blad pressure, hisertension or stroke jaise khatre bhi saamne aate hai

 Kanakaiah's grandmother told NDTV that we have not seen this kind of drought in my entire life
